Nothing will content them but the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC65" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="65" style="position:relative">extremest limit of the land; loitering under the shady lee of yonder</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC66" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="66" style="position:relative">warehouses will not suffice. No. They must get just as nigh the water</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC67" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="67" style="position:relative">as they possibly can without falling in. And there they stand—miles of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC68" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="68" style="position:relative">them—leagues. Inlanders all, they come from lanes and alleys, streets</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC69" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="69" style="position:relative">and avenues—north, east, south, and west. Yet here they all unite. Tell</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC70" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="70" style="position:relative">me, does the magnetic virtue of the needles of the compasses of all</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC71" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="71" style="position:relative">those ships attract them thither?</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC72" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="72" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC73" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="73" style="position:relative">Once more. Say you are in the country; in some high land of lakes. Take</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC74" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="74" style="position:relative">almost any path you please, and ten to one it carries you down in a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC75" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="75" style="position:relative">dale, and leaves you there by a pool in the stream. There is magic in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC76" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="76" style="position:relative">it. Let the most absent-minded of men be plunged in his deepest</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC77" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="77" style="position:relative">reveries—stand that man on his legs, set his feet a-going, and he will</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC78" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="78" style="position:relative">infallibly lead you to water, if water there be in all that region.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC79" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="79" style="position:relative">Should you ever be athirst in the great American desert, try this</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC80" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="80" style="position:relative">experiment, if your caravan happen to be supplied with a metaphysical</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC81" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="81" style="position:relative">professor. Yes, as every one knows, meditation and water are wedded for</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC82" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="82" style="position:relative">ever.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC83" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="83" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC84" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="84" style="position:relative">But here is an artist. He desires to paint you the dreamiest, shadiest,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC85" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="85" style="position:relative">quietest, most enchanting bit of romantic landscape in all the valley</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC86" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="86" style="position:relative">of the Saco. What is the chief element he employs? There stand his</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC87" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="87" style="position:relative">trees, each with a hollow trunk, as if a hermit and a crucifix were</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC88" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="88" style="position:relative">within; and here sleeps his meadow, and there sleep his cattle; and up</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC89" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="89" style="position:relative">from yonder cottage goes a sleepy smoke. Deep into distant woodlands</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC90" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="90" style="position:relative">winds a mazy way, reaching to overlapping spurs of mountains bathed in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC91" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="91" style="position:relative">their hill-side blue. But though the picture lies thus tranced, and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC92" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="92" style="position:relative">though this pine-tree shakes down its sighs like leaves upon this</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC93" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="93" style="position:relative">shepherd’s head, yet all were vain, unless the shepherd’s eye were</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC94" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="94" style="position:relative">fixed upon the magic stream before him. Go visit the Prairies in June,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC95" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="95" style="position:relative">when for scores on scores of miles you wade knee-deep among</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC96" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="96" style="position:relative">Tiger-lilies—what is the one charm wanting?—Water—there is not a drop</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC97" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="97" style="position:relative">of water there! Were Niagara but a cataract of sand, would you travel</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC98" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="98" style="position:relative">your thousand miles to see it? Why did the poor poet of Tennessee, upon</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC99" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="99" style="position:relative">suddenly receiving two handfuls of silver, deliberate whether to buy</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC100" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="100" style="position:relative">him a coat, which he sadly needed, or invest his money in a pedestrian</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC101" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="101" style="position:relative">trip to Rockaway Beach? Why is almost every robust healthy boy with a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC102" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="102" style="position:relative">robust healthy soul in him, at some time or other crazy to go to sea?</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC103" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="103" style="position:relative">Why upon your first voyage as a passenger, did you yourself feel such a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC104" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="104" style="position:relative">mystical vibration, when first told that you and your ship were now out</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC105" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="105" style="position:relative">of sight of land? Why did the old Persians hold the sea holy? Why did</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC106" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="106" style="position:relative">the Greeks give it a separate deity, and own brother of Jove? Surely</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC107" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="107" style="position:relative">all this is not without meaning. And still deeper the meaning of that</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC108" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="108" style="position:relative">story of Narcissus, who because he could not grasp the tormenting, mild</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC109" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="109" style="position:relative">image he saw in the fountain, plunged into it and was drowned. But that</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC110" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="110" style="position:relative">same image, we ourselves see in all rivers and oceans. It is the image</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC111" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="111" style="position:relative">of the ungraspable phantom of life; and this is the key to it all.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC112" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="112" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC113" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="113" style="position:relative">Now, when I say that I am in the habit of going to sea whenever I begin</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC114" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="114" style="position:relative">to grow hazy about the eyes, and begin to be over conscious of my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC115" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="115" style="position:relative">lungs, I do not mean to have it inferred that I ever go to sea as a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC116" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="116" style="position:relative">passenger. For to go as a passenger you must needs have a purse, and a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC117" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="117" style="position:relative">purse is but a rag unless you have something in it. Besides, passengers</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC118" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="118" style="position:relative">get sea-sick—grow quarrelsome—don’t sleep of nights—do not enjoy</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC119" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="119" style="position:relative">themselves much, as a general thing;—no, I never go as a passenger;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC120" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="120" style="position:relative">nor, though I am something of a salt, do I ever go to sea as a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC121" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="121" style="position:relative">Commodore, or a Captain, or a Cook. I abandon the glory and distinction</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC122" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="122" style="position:relative">of such offices to those who like them. For my part, I abominate all</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC123" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="123" style="position:relative">honorable respectable toils, trials, and tribulations of every kind</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC124" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="124" style="position:relative">whatsoever. It is quite as much as I can do to take care of myself,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC125" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="125" style="position:relative">without taking care of ships, barques, brigs, schooners, and what not.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC126" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="126" style="position:relative">And as for going as cook,—though I confess there is considerable glory</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC127" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="127" style="position:relative">in that, a cook being a sort of officer on ship-board—yet, somehow, I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC128" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="128" style="position:relative">never fancied broiling fowls;—though once broiled, judiciously</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC129" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="129" style="position:relative">buttered, and judgmatically salted and peppered, there is no one who</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC130" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="130" style="position:relative">will speak more respectfully, not to say reverentially, of a broiled</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC131" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="131" style="position:relative">fowl than I will. It is out of the idolatrous dotings of the old</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC132" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="132" style="position:relative">Egyptians upon broiled ibis and roasted river horse, that you see the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC133" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="133" style="position:relative">mummies of those creatures in their huge bake-houses the pyramids.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC134" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="134" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC135" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="135" style="position:relative">No, when I go to sea, I go as a simple sailor, right before the mast,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC136" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="136" style="position:relative">plumb down into the forecastle, aloft there to the royal mast-head.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC137" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="137" style="position:relative">True, they rather order me about some, and make me jump from spar to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC138" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="138" style="position:relative">spar, like a grasshopper in a May meadow. And at first, this sort of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC139" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="139" style="position:relative">thing is unpleasant enough. It touches one’s sense of honor,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC140" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="140" style="position:relative">particularly if you come of an old established family in the land, the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC141" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="141" style="position:relative">Van Rensselaers, or Randolphs, or Hardicanutes. And more than all, if</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC142" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="142" style="position:relative">just previous to putting your hand into the tar-pot, you have been</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC143" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="143" style="position:relative">lording it as a country schoolmaster, making the tallest boys stand in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC144" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="144" style="position:relative">awe of you. The transition is a keen one, I assure you, from a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC145" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="145" style="position:relative">schoolmaster to a sailor, and requires a strong decoction of Seneca and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC146" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="146" style="position:relative">the Stoics to enable you to grin and bear it. But even this wears off</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC147" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="147" style="position:relative">in time.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC148" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="148" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC149" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="149" style="position:relative">What of it, if some old hunks of a sea-captain orders me to get a broom</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC150" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="150" style="position:relative">and sweep down the decks? What does that indignity amount to, weighed,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC151" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="151" style="position:relative">I mean, in the scales of the New Testament? Do you think the archangel</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC152" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="152" style="position:relative">Gabriel thinks anything the less of me, because I promptly and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC153" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="153" style="position:relative">respectfully obey that old hunks in that particular instance? Who ain’t</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC154" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="154" style="position:relative">a slave? Tell me that. Well, then, however the old sea-captains may</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC155" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="155" style="position:relative">order me about—however they may thump and punch me about, I have the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC156" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="156" style="position:relative">satisfaction of knowing that it is all right; that everybody else is</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC157" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="157" style="position:relative">one way or other served in much the same way—either in a physical or</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC158" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="158" style="position:relative">metaphysical point of view, that is; and so the universal thump is</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC159" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="159" style="position:relative">passed round, and all hands should rub each other’s shoulder-blades,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC160" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="160" style="position:relative">and be content.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC161" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="161" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC162" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="162" style="position:relative">Again, I always go to sea as a sailor, because they make a point of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC163" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="163" style="position:relative">paying me for my trouble, whereas they never pay passengers a single</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC164" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="164" style="position:relative">penny that I ever heard of. On the contrary, passengers themselves must</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC165" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="165" style="position:relative">pay. And there is all the difference in the world between paying and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC166" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="166" style="position:relative">being paid. The act of paying is perhaps the most uncomfortable</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC167" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="167" style="position:relative">infliction that the two orchard thieves entailed upon us. But _being</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC168" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="168" style="position:relative">paid_,—what will compare with it? The urbane activity with which a man</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC169" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="169" style="position:relative">receives money is really marvellous, considering that we so earnestly</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC170" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="170" style="position:relative">believe money to be the root of all earthly ills, and that on no</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC171" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="171" style="position:relative">account can a monied man enter heaven. Ah! how cheerfully we consign</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC172" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="172" style="position:relative">ourselves to perdition!</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC173" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="173" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC174" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="174" style="position:relative">Finally, I always go to sea as a sailor, because of the wholesome</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC175" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="175" style="position:relative">exercise and pure air of the fore-castle deck. For as in this world,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC176" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="176" style="position:relative">head winds are far more prevalent than winds from astern (that is, if</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC177" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="177" style="position:relative">you never violate the Pythagorean maxim), so for the most part the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC178" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="178" style="position:relative">Commodore on the quarter-deck gets his atmosphere at second hand from</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC179" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="179" style="position:relative">the sailors on the forecastle. He thinks he breathes it first; but not</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC180" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="180" style="position:relative">so. In much the same way do the commonalty lead their leaders in many</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC181" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="181" style="position:relative">other things, at the same time that the leaders little suspect it. But</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC182" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="182" style="position:relative">wherefore it was that after having repeatedly smelt the sea as a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC183" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="183" style="position:relative">merchant sailor, I should now take it into my head to go on a whaling</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC184" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="184" style="position:relative">voyage; this the invisible police officer of the Fates, who has the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC185" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="185" style="position:relative">constant surveillance of me, and secretly dogs me, and influences me in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC186" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="186" style="position:relative">some unaccountable way—he can better answer than any one else. And,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC187" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="187" style="position:relative">doubtless, my going on this whaling voyage, formed part of the grand</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC188" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="188" style="position:relative">programme of Providence that was drawn up a long time ago. It came in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC189" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="189" style="position:relative">as a sort of brief interlude and solo between more extensive</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC190" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="190" style="position:relative">performances. I take it that this part of the bill must have run</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC191" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="191" style="position:relative">something like this:</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC192" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="192" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC193" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="193" style="position:relative">“_Grand Contested Election for the Presidency of the United States._</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC194" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="194" style="position:relative">“WHALING VOYAGE BY ONE ISHMAEL. “BLOODY BATTLE IN AFFGHANISTAN.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC195" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="195" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC196" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="196" style="position:relative">Though I cannot tell why it was exactly that those stage managers, the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC197" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="197" style="position:relative">Fates, put me down for this shabby part of a whaling voyage, when</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC198" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="198" style="position:relative">others were set down for magnificent parts in high tragedies, and short</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC199" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="199" style="position:relative">and easy parts in genteel comedies, and jolly parts in farces—though I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC200" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="200" style="position:relative">cannot tell why this was exactly; yet, now that I recall all the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC201" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="201" style="position:relative">circumstances, I think I can see a little into the springs and motives</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC202" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="202" style="position:relative">which being cunningly presented to me under various disguises, induced</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC203" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="203" style="position:relative">me to set about performing the part I did, besides cajoling me into the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC204" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="204" style="position:relative">delusion that it was a choice resulting from my own unbiased freewill</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC205" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="205" style="position:relative">and discriminating judgment.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC206" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="206" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC207" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="207" style="position:relative">Chief among these motives was the overwhelming idea of the great whale</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC208" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="208" style="position:relative">himself. Such a portentous and mysterious monster roused all my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC209" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="209" style="position:relative">curiosity. Then the wild and distant seas where he rolled his island</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC210" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="210" style="position:relative">bulk; the undeliverable, nameless perils of the whale; these, with all</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC211" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="211" style="position:relative">the attending marvels of a thousand Patagonian sights and sounds,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC212" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="212" style="position:relative">helped to sway me to my wish. With other men, perhaps, such things</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC213" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="213" style="position:relative">would not have been inducements; but as for me, I am tormented with an</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC214" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="214" style="position:relative">everlasting itch for things remote. I love to sail forbidden seas, and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC215" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="215" style="position:relative">land on barbarous coasts. Not ignoring what is good, I am quick to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC216" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="216" style="position:relative">perceive a horror, and could still be social with it—would they let</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC217" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="217" style="position:relative">me—since it is but well to be on friendly terms with all the inmates of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC218" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="218" style="position:relative">the place one lodges in.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC219" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="219" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC220" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="220" style="position:relative">By reason of these things, then, the whaling voyage was welcome; the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC221" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="221" style="position:relative">great flood-gates of the wonder-world swung open, and in the wild</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC222" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="222" style="position:relative">conceits that swayed me to my purpose, two and two there floated into</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC223" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="223" style="position:relative">my inmost soul, endless processions of the whale, and, mid most of them</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC224" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="224" style="position:relative">all, one grand hooded phantom, like a snow hill in the air.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC225" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="225" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC226" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="226" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC227" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="227" style="position:relative">CHAPTER 2. The Carpet-Bag.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC228" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="228" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC229" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="229" style="position:relative">I stuffed a shirt or two into my old carpet-bag, tucked it under my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC230" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="230" style="position:relative">arm, and started for Cape Horn and the Pacific. Quitting the good city</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC231" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="231" style="position:relative">of old Manhatto, I duly arrived in New Bedford. It was a Saturday night</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC232" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="232" style="position:relative">in December. Much was I disappointed upon learning that the little</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC233" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="233" style="position:relative">packet for Nantucket had already sailed, and that no way of reaching</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC234" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="234" style="position:relative">that place would offer, till the following Monday.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC235" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="235" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC236" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="236" style="position:relative">As most young candidates for the pains and penalties of whaling stop at</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC237" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="237" style="position:relative">this same New Bedford, thence to embark on their voyage, it may as well</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC238" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="238" style="position:relative">be related that I, for one, had no idea of so doing. For my mind was</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC239" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="239" style="position:relative">made up to sail in no other than a Nantucket craft, because there was a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC240" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="240" style="position:relative">fine, boisterous something about everything connected with that famous</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC241" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="241" style="position:relative">old island, which amazingly pleased me. Besides though New Bedford has</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC242" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="242" style="position:relative">of late been gradually monopolising the business of whaling, and though</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC243" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="243" style="position:relative">in this matter poor old Nantucket is now much behind her, yet Nantucket</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC244" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="244" style="position:relative">was her great original—the Tyre of this Carthage;—the place where the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC245" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="245" style="position:relative">first dead American whale was stranded. Where else but from Nantucket</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC246" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="246" style="position:relative">did those aboriginal whalemen, the Red-Men, first sally out in canoes</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC247" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="247" style="position:relative">to give chase to the Leviathan? And where but from Nantucket, too, did</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC248" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="248" style="position:relative">that first adventurous little sloop put forth, partly laden with</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC249" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="249" style="position:relative">imported cobblestones—so goes the story—to throw at the whales, in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC250" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="250" style="position:relative">order to discover when they were nigh enough to risk a harpoon from the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC251" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="251" style="position:relative">bowsprit?</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC252" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="252" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC253" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="253" style="position:relative">Now having a night, a day, and still another night following before me</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC254" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="254" style="position:relative">in New Bedford, ere I could embark for my destined port, it became a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC255" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="255" style="position:relative">matter of concernment where I was to eat and sleep meanwhile. It was a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC256" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="256" style="position:relative">very dubious-looking, nay, a very dark and dismal night, bitingly cold</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC257" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="257" style="position:relative">and cheerless. I knew no one in the place. With anxious grapnels I had</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC258" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="258" style="position:relative">sounded my pocket, and only brought up a few pieces of silver,—So,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC259" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="259" style="position:relative">wherever you go, Ishmael, said I to myself, as I stood in the middle of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC260" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="260" style="position:relative">a dreary street shouldering my bag, and comparing the gloom towards the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC261" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="261" style="position:relative">north with the darkness towards the south—wherever in your wisdom you</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC262" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="262" style="position:relative">may conclude to lodge for the night, my dear Ishmael, be sure to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC263" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="263" style="position:relative">inquire the price, and don’t be too particular.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC264" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="264" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC265" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="265" style="position:relative">With halting steps I paced the streets, and passed the sign of “The</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC266" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="266" style="position:relative">Crossed Harpoons”—but it looked too expensive and jolly there. Further</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC267" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="267" style="position:relative">on, from the bright red windows of the “Sword-Fish Inn,” there came</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC268" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="268" style="position:relative">such fervent rays, that it seemed to have melted the packed snow and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC269" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="269" style="position:relative">ice from before the house, for everywhere else the congealed frost lay</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC270" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="270" style="position:relative">ten inches thick in a hard, asphaltic pavement,—rather weary for me,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC271" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="271" style="position:relative">when I struck my foot against the flinty projections, because from</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC272" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="272" style="position:relative">hard, remorseless service the soles of my boots were in a most</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC273" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="273" style="position:relative">miserable plight. Too expensive and jolly, again thought I, pausing one</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC274" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="274" style="position:relative">moment to watch the broad glare in the street, and hear the sounds of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC275" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="275" style="position:relative">the tinkling glasses within. But go on, Ishmael, said I at last; don’t</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC276" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="276" style="position:relative">you hear? get away from before the door; your patched boots are</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC277" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="277" style="position:relative">stopping the way. So on I went. I now by instinct followed the streets</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC278" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="278" style="position:relative">that took me waterward, for there, doubtless, were the cheapest, if not</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC279" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="279" style="position:relative">the cheeriest inns.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC280" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="280" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC281" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="281" style="position:relative">Such dreary streets! blocks of blackness, not houses, on either hand,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC282" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="282" style="position:relative">and here and there a candle, like a candle moving about in a tomb. At</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC283" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="283" style="position:relative">this hour of the night, of the last day of the week, that quarter of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC284" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="284" style="position:relative">the town proved all but deserted. But presently I came to a smoky light</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC285" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="285" style="position:relative">proceeding from a low, wide building, the door of which stood</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC286" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="286" style="position:relative">invitingly open. It had a careless look, as if it were meant for the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC287" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="287" style="position:relative">uses of the public; so, entering, the first thing I did was to stumble</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC288" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="288" style="position:relative">over an ash-box in the porch. Ha! thought I, ha, as the flying</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC289" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="289" style="position:relative">particles almost choked me, are these ashes from that destroyed city,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC290" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="290" style="position:relative">Gomorrah? But “The Crossed Harpoons,” and “The Sword-Fish?”—this, then</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC291" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="291" style="position:relative">must needs be the sign of “The Trap.” However, I picked myself up and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC292" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="292" style="position:relative">hearing a loud voice within, pushed on and opened a second, interior</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC293" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="293" style="position:relative">door.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC294" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="294" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC295" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="295" style="position:relative">It seemed the great Black Parliament sitting in Tophet. A hundred black</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC296" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="296" style="position:relative">faces turned round in their rows to peer; and beyond, a black Angel of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC297" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="297" style="position:relative">Doom was beating a book in a pulpit. It was a negro church; and the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC298" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="298" style="position:relative">preacher’s text was about the blackness of darkness, and the weeping</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC299" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="299" style="position:relative">and wailing and teeth-gnashing there. Ha, Ishmael, muttered I, backing</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC300" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="300" style="position:relative">out, Wretched entertainment at the sign of ‘The Trap!’</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC301" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="301" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC302" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="302" style="position:relative">Moving on, I at last came to a dim sort of light not far from the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC303" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="303" style="position:relative">docks, and heard a forlorn creaking in the air; and looking up, saw a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC304" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="304" style="position:relative">swinging sign over the door with a white painting upon it, faintly</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC305" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="305" style="position:relative">representing a tall straight jet of misty spray, and these words</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC306" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="306" style="position:relative">underneath—“The Spouter Inn:—Peter Coffin.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC307" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="307" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC308" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="308" style="position:relative">Coffin?—Spouter?—Rather ominous in that particular connexion, thought</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC309" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="309" style="position:relative">I. But it is a common name in Nantucket, they say, and I suppose this</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC310" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="310" style="position:relative">Peter here is an emigrant from there. As the light looked so dim, and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC311" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="311" style="position:relative">the place, for the time, looked quiet enough, and the dilapidated</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC312" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="312" style="position:relative">little wooden house itself looked as if it might have been carted here</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC313" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="313" style="position:relative">from the ruins of some burnt district, and as the swinging sign had a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC314" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="314" style="position:relative">poverty-stricken sort of creak to it, I thought that here was the very</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC315" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="315" style="position:relative">spot for cheap lodgings, and the best of pea coffee.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC316" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="316" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC317" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="317" style="position:relative">It was a queer sort of place—a gable-ended old house, one side palsied</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC318" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="318" style="position:relative">as it were, and leaning over sadly. It stood on a sharp bleak corner,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC319" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="319" style="position:relative">where that tempestuous wind Euroclydon kept up a worse howling than</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC320" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="320" style="position:relative">ever it did about poor Paul’s tossed craft. Euroclydon, nevertheless,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC321" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="321" style="position:relative">is a mighty pleasant zephyr to any one in-doors, with his feet on the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC322" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="322" style="position:relative">hob quietly toasting for bed. “In judging of that tempestuous wind</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC323" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="323" style="position:relative">called Euroclydon,” says an old writer—of whose works I possess the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC324" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="324" style="position:relative">only copy extant—“it maketh a marvellous difference, whether thou</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC325" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="325" style="position:relative">lookest out at it from a glass window where the frost is all on the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC326" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="326" style="position:relative">outside, or whether thou observest it from that sashless window, where</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC327" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="327" style="position:relative">the frost is on both sides, and of which the wight Death is the only</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC328" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="328" style="position:relative">glazier.” True enough, thought I, as this passage occurred to my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC329" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="329" style="position:relative">mind—old black-letter, thou reasonest well. Yes, these eyes are</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC330" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="330" style="position:relative">windows, and this body of mine is the house. What a pity they didn’t</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC331" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="331" style="position:relative">stop up the chinks and the crannies though, and thrust in a little lint</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC332" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="332" style="position:relative">here and there. But it’s too late to make any improvements now. The</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC333" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="333" style="position:relative">universe is finished; the copestone is on, and the chips were carted</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC334" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="334" style="position:relative">off a million years ago. Poor Lazarus there, chattering his teeth</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC335" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="335" style="position:relative">against the curbstone for his pillow, and shaking off his tatters with</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC336" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="336" style="position:relative">his shiverings, he might plug up both ears with rags, and put a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC337" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="337" style="position:relative">corn-cob into his mouth, and yet that would not keep out the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC338" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="338" style="position:relative">tempestuous Euroclydon. Euroclydon! says old Dives, in his red silken</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC339" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="339" style="position:relative">wrapper—(he had a redder one afterwards) pooh, pooh! What a fine frosty</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC340" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="340" style="position:relative">night; how Orion glitters; what northern lights! Let them talk of their</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC341" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="341" style="position:relative">oriental summer climes of everlasting conservatories; give me the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC342" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="342" style="position:relative">privilege of making my own summer with my own coals.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC343" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="343" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC344" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="344" style="position:relative">But what thinks Lazarus? Can he warm his blue hands by holding them up</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC345" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="345" style="position:relative">to the grand northern lights? Would not Lazarus rather be in Sumatra</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC346" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="346" style="position:relative">than here?
