I sang out, I could not help it</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC874" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="874" style="position:relative">now; and giving a sudden grunt of astonishment he began feeling me.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC875" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="875" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC876" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="876" style="position:relative">Stammering out something, I knew not what, I rolled away from him</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC877" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="877" style="position:relative">against the wall, and then conjured him, whoever or whatever he might</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC878" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="878" style="position:relative">be, to keep quiet, and let me get up and light the lamp again. But his</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC879" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="879" style="position:relative">guttural responses satisfied me at once that he but ill comprehended my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC880" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="880" style="position:relative">meaning.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC881" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="881" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC882" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="882" style="position:relative">“Who-e debel you?”—he at last said—“you no speak-e, dam-me, I kill-e.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC883" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="883" style="position:relative">And so saying the lighted tomahawk began flourishing about me in the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC884" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="884" style="position:relative">dark.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC885" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="885" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC886" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="886" style="position:relative">“Landlord, for God’s sake, Peter Coffin!” shouted I. “Landlord! Watch!</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC887" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="887" style="position:relative">Coffin! Angels! save me!”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC888" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="888" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC889" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="889" style="position:relative">“Speak-e! tell-ee me who-ee be, or dam-me, I kill-e!” again growled the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC890" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="890" style="position:relative">cannibal, while his horrid flourishings of the tomahawk scattered the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC891" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="891" style="position:relative">hot tobacco ashes about me till I thought my linen would get on fire.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC892" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="892" style="position:relative">But thank heaven, at that moment the landlord came into the room light</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC893" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="893" style="position:relative">in hand, and leaping from the bed I ran up to him.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC894" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="894" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC895" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="895" style="position:relative">“Don’t be afraid now,” said he, grinning again, “Queequeg here wouldn’t</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC896" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="896" style="position:relative">harm a hair of your head.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC897" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="897" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC898" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="898" style="position:relative">“Stop your grinning,” shouted I, “and why didn’t you tell me that that</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC899" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="899" style="position:relative">infernal harpooneer was a cannibal?”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC900" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="900" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC901" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="901" style="position:relative">“I thought ye know’d it;—didn’t I tell ye, he was a peddlin’ heads</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC902" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="902" style="position:relative">around town?—but turn flukes again and go to sleep. Queequeg, look</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC903" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="903" style="position:relative">here—you sabbee me, I sabbee—you this man sleepe you—you sabbee?”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC904" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="904" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC905" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="905" style="position:relative">“Me sabbee plenty”—grunted Queequeg, puffing away at his pipe and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC906" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="906" style="position:relative">sitting up in bed.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC907" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="907" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC908" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="908" style="position:relative">“You gettee in,” he added, motioning to me with his tomahawk, and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC909" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="909" style="position:relative">throwing the clothes to one side. He really did this in not only a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC910" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="910" style="position:relative">civil but a really kind and charitable way. I stood looking at him a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC911" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="911" style="position:relative">moment. For all his tattooings he was on the whole a clean, comely</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC912" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="912" style="position:relative">looking cannibal. What’s all this fuss I have been making about,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC913" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="913" style="position:relative">thought I to myself—the man’s a human being just as I am: he has just</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC914" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="914" style="position:relative">as much reason to fear me, as I have to be afraid of him. Better sleep</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC915" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="915" style="position:relative">with a sober cannibal than a drunken Christian.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC916" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="916" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC917" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="917" style="position:relative">“Landlord,” said I, “tell him to stash his tomahawk there, or pipe, or</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC918" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="918" style="position:relative">whatever you call it; tell him to stop smoking, in short, and I will</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC919" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="919" style="position:relative">turn in with him. But I don’t fancy having a man smoking in bed with</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC920" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="920" style="position:relative">me. It’s dangerous. Besides, I ain’t insured.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC921" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="921" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC922" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="922" style="position:relative">This being told to Queequeg, he at once complied, and again politely</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC923" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="923" style="position:relative">motioned me to get into bed—rolling over to one side as much as to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC924" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="924" style="position:relative">say—“I won’t touch a leg of ye.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC925" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="925" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC926" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="926" style="position:relative">“Good night, landlord,” said I, “you may go.”</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC927" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="927" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC928" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="928" style="position:relative">I turned in, and never slept better in my life.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC929" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="929" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC930" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="930" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC931" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="931" style="position:relative">CHAPTER 4. The Counterpane.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC932" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="932" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC933" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="933" style="position:relative">Upon waking next morning about daylight, I found Queequeg’s arm thrown</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC934" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="934" style="position:relative">over me in the most loving and affectionate manner. You had almost</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC935" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="935" style="position:relative">thought I had been his wife. The counterpane was of patchwork, full of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC936" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="936" style="position:relative">odd little parti-coloured squares and triangles; and this arm of his</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC937" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="937" style="position:relative">tattooed all over with an interminable Cretan labyrinth of a figure, no</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC938" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="938" style="position:relative">two parts of which were of one precise shade—owing I suppose to his</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC939" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="939" style="position:relative">keeping his arm at sea unmethodically in sun and shade, his shirt</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC940" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="940" style="position:relative">sleeves irregularly rolled up at various times—this same arm of his, I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC941" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="941" style="position:relative">say, looked for all the world like a strip of that same patchwork</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC942" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="942" style="position:relative">quilt. Indeed, partly lying on it as the arm did when I first awoke, I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC943" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="943" style="position:relative">could hardly tell it from the quilt, they so blended their hues</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC944" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="944" style="position:relative">together; and it was only by the sense of weight and pressure that I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC945" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="945" style="position:relative">could tell that Queequeg was hugging me.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC946" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="946" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC947" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="947" style="position:relative">My sensations were strange. Let me try to explain them. When I was a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC948" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="948" style="position:relative">child, I well remember a somewhat similar circumstance that befell me;</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC949" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="949" style="position:relative">whether it was a reality or a dream, I never could entirely settle. The</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC950" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="950" style="position:relative">circumstance was this. I had been cutting up some caper or other—I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC951" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="951" style="position:relative">think it was trying to crawl up the chimney, as I had seen a little</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC952" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="952" style="position:relative">sweep do a few days previous; and my stepmother who, somehow or other,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC953" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="953" style="position:relative">was all the time whipping me, or sending me to bed supperless,—my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC954" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="954" style="position:relative">mother dragged me by the legs out of the chimney and packed me off to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC955" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="955" style="position:relative">bed, though it was only two o’clock in the afternoon of the 21st June,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC956" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="956" style="position:relative">the longest day in the year in our hemisphere. I felt dreadfully. But</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC957" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="957" style="position:relative">there was no help for it, so up stairs I went to my little room in the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC958" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="958" style="position:relative">third floor, undressed myself as slowly as possible so as to kill time,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC959" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="959" style="position:relative">and with a bitter sigh got between the sheets.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC960" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="960" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC961" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="961" style="position:relative">I lay there dismally calculating that sixteen entire hours must elapse</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC962" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="962" style="position:relative">before I could hope for a resurrection. Sixteen hours in bed! the small</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC963" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="963" style="position:relative">of my back ached to think of it. And it was so light too; the sun</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC964" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="964" style="position:relative">shining in at the window, and a great rattling of coaches in the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC965" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="965" style="position:relative">streets, and the sound of gay voices all over the house. I felt worse</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC966" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="966" style="position:relative">and worse—at last I got up, dressed, and softly going down in my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC967" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="967" style="position:relative">stockinged feet, sought out my stepmother, and suddenly threw myself at</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC968" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="968" style="position:relative">her feet, beseeching her as a particular favour to give me a good</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC969" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="969" style="position:relative">slippering for my misbehaviour; anything indeed but condemning me to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC970" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="970" style="position:relative">lie abed such an unendurable length of time. But she was the best and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC971" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="971" style="position:relative">most conscientious of stepmothers, and back I had to go to my room. For</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC972" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="972" style="position:relative">several hours I lay there broad awake, feeling a great deal worse than</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC973" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="973" style="position:relative">I have ever done since, even from the greatest subsequent misfortunes.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC974" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="974" style="position:relative">At last I must have fallen into a troubled nightmare of a doze; and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC975" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="975" style="position:relative">slowly waking from it—half steeped in dreams—I opened my eyes, and the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC976" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="976" style="position:relative">before sun-lit room was now wrapped in outer darkness. Instantly I felt</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC977" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="977" style="position:relative">a shock running through all my frame; nothing was to be seen, and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC978" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="978" style="position:relative">nothing was to be heard; but a supernatural hand seemed placed in mine.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC979" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="979" style="position:relative">My arm hung over the counterpane, and the nameless, unimaginable,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC980" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="980" style="position:relative">silent form or phantom, to which the hand belonged, seemed closely</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC981" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="981" style="position:relative">seated by my bed-side. For what seemed ages piled on ages, I lay there,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC982" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="982" style="position:relative">frozen with the most awful fears, not daring to drag away my hand; yet</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC983" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="983" style="position:relative">ever thinking that if I could but stir it one single inch, the horrid</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC984" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="984" style="position:relative">spell would be broken. I knew not how this consciousness at last glided</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC985" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="985" style="position:relative">away from me; but waking in the morning, I shudderingly remembered it</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC986" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="986" style="position:relative">all, and for days and weeks and months afterwards I lost myself in</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC987" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="987" style="position:relative">confounding attempts to explain the mystery. Nay, to this very hour, I</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC988" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="988" style="position:relative">often puzzle myself with it.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC989" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="989" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC990" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="990" style="position:relative">Now, take away the awful fear, and my sensations at feeling the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC991" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="991" style="position:relative">supernatural hand in mine were very similar, in their strangeness, to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC992" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="992" style="position:relative">those which I experienced on waking up and seeing Queequeg’s pagan arm</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC993" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="993" style="position:relative">thrown round me. But at length all the past night’s events soberly</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC994" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="994" style="position:relative">recurred, one by one, in fixed reality, and then I lay only alive to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC995" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="995" style="position:relative">the comical predicament. For though I tried to move his arm—unlock his</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC996" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="996" style="position:relative">bridegroom clasp—yet, sleeping as he was, he still hugged me tightly,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC997" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="997" style="position:relative">as though naught but death should part us twain. I now strove to rouse</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC998" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="998" style="position:relative">him—“Queequeg!”—but his only answer was a snore. I then rolled over, my</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC999" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="999" style="position:relative">neck feeling as if it were in a horse-collar; and suddenly felt a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC1000" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="1000" style="position:relative">slight scratch. Throwing aside the counterpane, there lay the tomahawk</div></div></div></div></div><div class="CodeLinesSSR-module__viewRemainderLink__pd3EU"><a class="prc-Link-Link-9ZwDx" href="https://github.com/roberto-inf/building-llm-applications/raw/refs/heads/main/ch03/Moby-Dick.txt">View remainder of file in raw view</a></div></div><div id="copilot-button-container"></div></div><div id="highlighted-line-menu-container"></div></div></div><button hidden="" data-testid="hotkey-button" data-hotkey-scope="read-only-cursor-text-area"></button><button hidden=""></button></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><button hidden="" data-testid="" data-hotkey-scope="read-only-cursor-text-area"></button><button hidden=""></button></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_1___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"day"}</script></div>
